These results will test scaling ability of FDB

It's just not possible to get lower latency than this (it is measured in microseconds, however)

The possible situations:
. Single node vs multi-node
.. For single, 1x or 2x scale
.. For multi, 2 dc or 3 dc
.. For multi, 2 dc at 1x or 2 dc at 2x

All ycsb testing will be done with the exact same test scenarios, only FDB configuration will change
